                <script>
                    window.pbjs = window.pbjs || {}; pbjs.que = pbjs.que || [];
                    window.googletag = window.googletag || { cmd: [] };

                    var headerBiddingSlots = [];
                    var nonHeaderBiddingSlots = [];

                    function sendAdServerRequest(slots) {
                        if (pbjs.adserverRequestSent) return;
                        pbjs.adserverRequestSent = true;

                        pbjs.setTargetingForGPTAsync();
                        googletag.cmd.push(function () {
                            googletag.pubads().refresh(slots);
                        });
                    }

                    googletag.cmd.push(function () {
                        // ------- Size mappings -------
                        var mappingMasthead = googletag.sizeMapping()
                            .addSize([1024, 0], [[970, 250], [970, 90]])
                            .addSize([768, 0], [[728, 90]])
                            .addSize([320, 0], [[320, 100], [320, 50]])
                            .build();

                        var mappingTopMREC = googletag.sizeMapping()
                            .addSize([768, 0], [[300, 250]])
                            .addSize([0, 0], []) // no mobile render
                            .build();

                        // Sidebar = desktop/tablet only
                        var mappingSidebar = googletag.sizeMapping()
                            .addSize([768, 0], [[300, 600], [300, 250]])
                            .addSize([0, 0], []) // no mobile render
                            .build();

                        // Anchor responsive
                        var mappingAnchor = googletag.sizeMapping()
                            .addSize([1024, 0], [[970, 90]])
                            .addSize([768, 0], [[728, 90]])
                            .addSize([320, 0], [[320, 50]])
                            .build();

                        // Mobile MREC = mobile only
                        var mappingMobileMREC = googletag.sizeMapping()
                            .addSize([768, 0], [])                 // no tablet/desktop
                            .addSize([320, 0], [[300, 250]])       // mobile
                            .build();

                        // ------- Define slots -------
                        headerBiddingSlots.push(
                            googletag.defineSlot('/135062774,22932914647/BarTV-Masthead', [[970, 250], [970, 90], [728, 90], [320, 100], [320, 50]], 'Masthead')
                                .defineSizeMapping(mappingMasthead)
                                .addService(googletag.pubads())
                        );

                        headerBiddingSlots.push(
                            googletag.defineSlot('/135062774,22932914647/BarTV-TopMREC', [[300, 250]], 'TopMREC')
                                .defineSizeMapping(mappingTopMREC)
                                .addService(googletag.pubads())
                        );

                        headerBiddingSlots.push(
                            googletag.defineSlot('/135062774,22932914647/BarTV-Sidebar', [[300, 600], [300, 250]], 'Sidebar')
                                .defineSizeMapping(mappingSidebar)
                                .addService(googletag.pubads())
                        );

                                
                                headerBiddingSlots.push(
                                    googletag.defineSlot('/135062774,22932914647/BarTV-MobileMREC', [[300, 250]], 'MobileMREC')
                                        .defineSizeMapping(mappingMobileMREC)
                                        .addService(googletag.pubads())
                                );

                        headerBiddingSlots.push(
                            googletag.defineSlot('/135062774,22932914647/BarTV-Anchor', [[970, 90], [728, 90], [320, 50]], 'Anchor')
                                .defineSizeMapping(mappingAnchor)
                                .addService(googletag.pubads())
                        );

                        // ------- GPT config -------
                        googletag.pubads().setCentering(true);
                        googletag.pubads().disableInitialLoad();       // <- critical for Prebid
                        googletag.pubads().enableSingleRequest();

                        // Optional page-level targeting (fill with real values when available)
                        googletag.pubads().setTargeting('postType', ['home']);
                        googletag.pubads().setTargeting('postID', ['1059']);
                        googletag.pubads().setTargeting('loggedIn', ['false']);
                        googletag.pubads().setTargeting('subscribed', ['false']);
                        googletag.pubads().setTargeting('sport', ['none']);


                        // Set if you truly need to override GPT's URL context
                        googletag.pubads().set('page_url', 'https://www.bartvsports.com.au/');
                        googletag.pubads().collapseEmptyDivs();
                        googletag.enableServices();

                        // Any non-HB slots? refresh them immediately
                        if (nonHeaderBiddingSlots.length > 0) {
                            googletag.pubads().refresh(nonHeaderBiddingSlots);
                        }

                        // ------- Prebid / Demand Manager -------
                        pbjs.que.push(function () {
                            pbjs.rp.requestBids({
                                callback: function () {
                                    sendAdServerRequest(headerBiddingSlots);
                                },
                                gptSlotObjects: headerBiddingSlots,
                                data: {
                                    inventory: {
                                        postType: ["home"],
                                        postID: ["1059"],
                                        loggedIn: ["false"],
                                        subscribed: ["false"]
                                    }
                                }
                            });
                        });

                        // Timeout safeguard
                        setTimeout(function () { sendAdServerRequest(headerBiddingSlots); }, 3000);
                    });
